99	        xmlns:xs="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema">
100	
101	    <wsdl:message name="myMessage">
102	        <wsdl:part name="content" type="xs:string"/>
103	    </wsdl:message>
104	
105	    <wsdl:portType name="myPortType">
106	        <wsdl:operation name="myOperation">
107	           <wsdl:input message="myMessage"/>
108	        </wsdl:operation>
109	    </wsdl:portType>
110	
111	    <wsdl:binding name="myBinding" type="myPortType">
112	        <wsdl:operation name="myOperation">
113	           <wsdl:input/>
114	        </wsdl:operation>
115	    </wsdl:binding>
116	
117	    <wsdl:service name="myService">
118	        <wsdl:port name="myPort" binding="myBinding"/>
119	    </wsdl:service>
120	
121	</wsdl:definitions>
